== Monorepo Packages ==
Packages: web (Next.js frontend), api (tRPC/Express backend), shared (types/schemas)

== Tech Stack ==
- Next.js 14 with App Router (packages/web)
- tRPC with Express adapter (packages/api)
- Prisma ORM with PostgreSQL (prisma/schema.prisma)
- Tailwind CSS for styling
- Turborepo for monorepo management
- TypeScript throughout

== Data Models (Prisma) ==
- Question: id, title, content, votes, answerCount, views, author, timestamps, soft-delete
- Answer: id, content, votes, accepted, author, linked to Question
- Tag: id, name (unique), many-to-many with Question

== API Routes ==
- questions.list: Returns all questions from in-memory store
- questions.search: Filters questions by title/content match

== Current Issues in Codebase ==
1. Search returns deleted posts (no deletedAt filter)
2. In-memory data store (not using Prisma/PostgreSQL)
3. No pagination on question list
4. No authentication implemented

== Dependencies Status ==
node_modules present - dependencies already installed
